Broker-Side Authentication Implementation\\n\\n### Overview\\nThe SASL broker-side authentication in Apache Kafka is implemented through a sophisticated system of classes that handle mechanism selection, server-side SASL protocol execution, and credential validation. The implementation supports multiple mechanisms: PLAIN, SCRAM (SHA-256/512), GSSAPI (Kerberos), and OAuthBearer.\\n\\n### Core Authentication Flow\\n\\n**SaslServerAuthenticator** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/SaslServerAuthenticator.java) is the central class implementing the Authenticator interface. It manages the entire broker-side SASL authentication lifecycle with defined state transitions:\\n- **INITIAL_REQUEST**: Initial state, expecting either ApiVersions or SaslHandshake request\\n- **HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST**: Can accept either ApiVersions or SaslHandshake\\n- **HANDSHAKE_REQUEST**: After ApiVersions, must receive SaslHandshake\\n- **AUTHENTICATE**: Authentication token exchange phase\\n- **COMPLETE**: Authentication succeeded\\n- **FAILED**: Authentication failed\\n- **REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE**: Re-authentication initiation state\\n\\nThe authenticate() method processes client requests through handleKafkaRequest() for initial handshake, then handleSaslToken() for authentication tokens.\\n\\n### Mechanism Selection and Creation\\n\\n**SaslChannelBuilder** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/SaslChannelBuilder.java) is responsible for configuring and selecting the appropriate callback handlers based on enabled SASL mechanisms. The createServerCallbackHandlers() method instantiates mechanism-specific handlers:\\n\\n1. **PLAIN**: PlainServerCallbackHandler (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/internals/PlainServerCallbackHandler.java)\\n2. **SCRAM**: ScramServerCallbackHandler (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramServerCallbackHandler.java)\\n3. **GSSAPI**: SaslServerCallbackHandler (default for Kerberos)\\n4. **OAuthBearer**: OAuthBearerUnsecuredValidatorCallbackHandler (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/oauthbearer/internals/unsecured/OAuthBearerUnsecuredValidatorCallbackHandler.java)\\n\\nThe handleHandshakeRequest() method in SaslServerAuthenticator validates the client-selected mechanism against the enabled mechanisms list and returns the list of supported mechanisms if validation fails.\\n\\n### Mechanism-Specific Implementations\\n\\n**PLAIN Mechanism**:\\n- PlainSaslServer (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/internals/PlainSaslServer.java): Implements SaslServer for PLAIN authentication\\n- PlainLoginModule (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/PlainLoginModule.java): JAAS login module for PLAIN\\n- PlainServerCallbackHandler: Handles username/password validation callbacks\\n\\n**SCRAM Mechanisms** (SCRAM-SHA-256, SCRAM-SHA-512):\\n- ScramSaslServer (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramSaslServer.java): Implements SaslServer for SCRAM authentication with salted password generation and multi-round authentication\\n- ScramServerCallbackHandler: Manages credential cache lookups for SCRAM credentials\\n- ScramLoginModule (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/ScramLoginModule.java): JAAS login module for SCRAM\\n- ScramMechanism (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramMechanism.java): Enum defining SCRAM mechanism variants and properties\\n\\n**GSSAPI (Kerberos)**:\\n- Handled through Broker-Side Authentication Implementation\\n\\n### Overview\\nThe SASL broker-side authentication in Apache Kafka is implemented through a sophisticated system of classes that handle mechanism selection, server-side SASL protocol execution, and credential validation. The implementation supports multiple mechanisms: PLAIN, SCRAM (SHA-256/512), GSSAPI (Kerberos), and OAuthBearer.\\n\\n### Core Authentication Flow\\n\\n**SaslServerAuthenticator** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/SaslServerAuthenticator.java) is the central class implementing the Authenticator interface. It manages the entire broker-side SASL authentication lifecycle with defined state transitions:\\n- **INITIAL_REQUEST**: Initial state, expecting either ApiVersions or SaslHandshake request\\n- **HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST**: Can accept either ApiVersions or SaslHandshake\\n- **HANDSHAKE_REQUEST**: After ApiVersions, must receive SaslHandshake\\n- **AUTHENTICATE**: Authentication token exchange phase\\n- **COMPLETE**: Authentication succeeded\\n- **FAILED**: Authentication failed\\n- **REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE**: Re-authentication initiation state\\n\\nThe authenticate() method processes client requests through handleKafkaRequest() for initial handshake, then handleSaslToken() for authentication tokens.\\n\\n### Mechanism Selection and Creation\\n\\n**SaslChannelBuilder** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/SaslChannelBuilder.java) is responsible for configuring and selecting the appropriate callback handlers based on enabled SASL mechanisms. The createServerCallbackHandlers() method instantiates mechanism-specific handlers:\\n\\n1. **PLAIN**: PlainServerCallbackHandler (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/internals/PlainServerCallbackHandler.java)\\n2. **SCRAM**: ScramServerCallbackHandler (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramServerCallbackHandler.java)\\n3. **GSSAPI**: SaslServerCallbackHandler (default for Kerberos)\\n4. **OAuthBearer**: fails.\\n\\n### Mechanism-Specific Implementations\\n\\n**PLAIN Mechanism**:\\n- PlainSaslServer (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/internals/PlainSaslServer.java):
